I've uploaded a python code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
target-allocator doesn't check if CRDs exist before querying them
### Component(s)

target allocator

### What happened?

## Description

We've got the case, where one of our clients is using a `target-allocator` on the cluster, where not all of `monitoring.coreos.com` CRDs are installed. They want to monitor only `ServiceMonitor` and `PodMonitor` resources, and don't want to monitor `Probe` and `ScrapeConfig` resources, since they didn't install them on the cluster.

What happens is that the target-allocator throws errors, still trying to query non-existent CRDs.

```

{"level":"info","ts":"2025-04-14T05:41:49Z","msg":"pkg/mod/k8s.io/client-go@v0.31.3/tools/cache/reflector.go:243: failed to list *v1alpha1.ScrapeConfig: the server could not find the requested resource (get scrapeconfigs.monitoring.coreos.com)"}
```

We're using a static config for target-allocator passed via ConfigMap, we don't use `OpenTelemetryCollector` CRD for it. While I was researching the issue, I've thought: maybe you just can't configure `Probe` and `ScrapeConfig` via YAML config yet – since I haven't seen it in the readme. So what I tried next is:

* creating `Probe` and `ScrapeConfig` CRDs in my test cluster, so they can be monitored by target-allocator
* disabling `PodMonitorSelector` and `ServiceMonitorSelector` that CAN be configured in static config
* deleting `PodMonitor` and `ServiceMonitor` CRDs from the cluster

And I've got the same error like the one I wrote above, this time it was about `PodMonitor` and `ServiceMonitor` CRDs that doesn't exist, even after I've disabled them.

Which means that target-allocator:

* queries all of 4 CRDs, no matter how you configure it
* doesn't check if CRDs exist, blindly relying on the idea that they exist

I don't think this is not how it should work, so I wanted to propose the idea to check if CRDs exist before querying them. If they don't exist, then print a WARN message and gracefully shutdown the monitoring of resources, CRDs of which don't exist.

If this idea gets a positive reaction, I can even try to implement the fix myself.

## Steps to Reproduce

* disabling `PodMonitorSelector` or `ServiceMonitorSelector` or any other selector that can be configured in static config
* deleting `PodMonitor` or `ServiceMonitor` or any other CRD from the cluster

## Expected Result

target-allocator doesn't query CRD of disabled resource selector

## Actual Result

target-allocator queries CRD of disabled resource selector and throws the error if there is no such CRD in the cluster

### Kubernetes Version

1.30.5

### Operator version

ghcr.io/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-operator/target-allocator:v0.124.0

### Collector version

ghcr.io/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-collector-releases/opentelemetry-collector-contrib:0.124.1

### Environment information

## Environment

this issue is relevant for all environments

    42	func NewPrometheusCRWatcher(
    43	        ctx context.Context,
    44	        logger logr.Logger,
    45	        client kubernetes.Interface,
    46	        monitoringclient monitoringclient.Interface,
    47	        cfg allocatorconfig.Config,
    48	) (*PrometheusCRWatcher, error) {
    49	        promLogger := slog.New(slog.NewTextHandler(os.Stderr, &slog.HandlerOptions{Level: slog.LevelWarn}))
    50	        slogger := slog.New(logr.ToSlogHandler(logger))
    51	        var resourceSelector *prometheus.ResourceSelector
    52	
    53	        allowList, denyList := cfg.PrometheusCR.GetAllowDenyLists()
    54	
    55	        factory := informers.NewMonitoringInformerFactories(allowList, denyList, monitoringclient, allocatorconfig.DefaultResyncTime, nil)
    56	
    57	        monitoringInformers, err := getInformers(factory)
    58	        if err != nil {
    59	                return nil, err
    60	        }
    61	
    62	        // we want to use endpointslices by default
    63	        serviceDiscoveryRole := monitoringv1.ServiceDiscoveryRole("EndpointSlice")
    64	
    65	        // TODO: We should make these durations configurable
    66	        prom := &monitoringv1.Prometheus{
    67	                ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
    68	                        Namespace: cfg.CollectorNamespace,
    69	                },
    70	                Spec: monitoringv1.PrometheusSpec{
    71	                        CommonPrometheusFields: monitoringv1.CommonPrometheusFields{

    73	                                PodMonitorSelector:              cfg.PrometheusCR.PodMonitorSelector,
    74	                                PodMonitorNamespaceSelector:     cfg.PrometheusCR.PodMonitorNamespaceSelector,
    75	                                ServiceMonitorSelector:          cfg.PrometheusCR.ServiceMonitorSelector,
    76	                                ServiceMonitorNamespaceSelector: cfg.PrometheusCR.ServiceMonitorNamespaceSelector,
    77	                                ScrapeConfigSelector:            cfg.PrometheusCR.ScrapeConfigSelector,
    78	                                ScrapeConfigNamespaceSelector:   cfg.PrometheusCR.ScrapeConfigNamespaceSelector,
    79	                                ProbeSelector:                   cfg.PrometheusCR.ProbeSelector,
    80	                                ProbeNamespaceSelector:          cfg.PrometheusCR.ProbeNamespaceSelector,
    81	                                ServiceDiscoveryRole:            &serviceDiscoveryRole,
    82	                                Version:                         "2.55.1", // fix Prometheus version 2 to avoid generating incompatible config
    83	                                ScrapeProtocols:                 cfg.PrometheusCR.ScrapeProtocols,
    84	                        },
    85	                        EvaluationInterval: monitoringv1.Duration("30s"),
    86	                },
    87	        }
    88	
    89	        generator, err := prometheus.NewConfigGenerator(promLogger, prom, prometheus.WithEndpointSliceSupport(), prometheus.WithInlineTLSConfig())
    90

    92	                return nil, err
    93	        }

    95	        store := assets.NewStoreBuilder(client.CoreV1(), client.CoreV1())
    96	        promRegisterer := prometheusgoclient.NewRegistry()
    97	        operatorMetrics := operator.NewMetrics(promRegisterer)
    98	        eventRecorderFactory := operator.NewEventRecorderFactory(false)
    99	        eventRecorder := eventRecorderFactory(client, "target-allocator")
   100	
   101	        var nsMonInf cache.SharedIndexInformer
   102	        getNamespaceInformerErr := retry.OnError(retry.DefaultRetry,
   103	                func(err error) bool {
   104	                        logger.Error(err, "Retrying namespace informer creation in promOperator CRD watcher")
   105	                        return true
   106	                }, func() error {
   107	                        nsMonInf, err = getNamespaceInformer(ctx, allowList, denyList, promLogger, client, operatorMetrics)
   108	                        return err
   109	                })
   110	        if getNamespaceInformerErr != nil {
   111	                logger.Error(getNamespaceInformerErr, "Failed to create namespace informer in promOperator CRD watcher")
   112	                return nil, getNamespaceInformerErr
   113	        }
   114	
   115	        resourceSelector, err = prometheus.NewResourceSelector(slogger, prom, store, nsMonInf, operatorMetrics, eventRecorder)
   116	        if err != nil {
   117	                logger.Error(err, "Failed to create resource selector in promOperator CRD watcher")
   118	        }
   119	
   120	        return &PrometheusCRWatcher{
   121	                logger:                          slogger,
   122	                kubeMonitoringClient:            monitoringclient,
   123	                k8sClient:                       client,
   124	                informers:                       monitoringInformers,
   125	                nsInformer:                      nsMonInf,
   126	                stopChannel:                     make(chan struct{}),
   127	                eventInterval:                   minEventInterval,
   128	                configGenerator:                 generator,
   129	                kubeConfigPath:                  cfg.KubeConfigFilePath,
   130	                podMonitorNamespaceSelector:     cfg.PrometheusCR.PodMonitorNamespaceSelector,
   131	                serviceMonitorNamespaceSelector: cfg.PrometheusCR.ServiceMonitorNamespaceSelector,
   132	                scrapeConfigNamespaceSelector:   cfg.PrometheusCR.ScrapeConfigNamespaceSelector,
   133	                probeNamespaceSelector:          cfg.PrometheusCR.ProbeNamespaceSelector,
   134	                resourceSelector:                resourceSelector,
   135	                store:                           store,
   136	                prometheusCR:                    prom,
   137	        }, nil
   138	}
   139	
   140	type PrometheusCRWatcher struct {
   141	        logger                          *slog.Logger
   142	        kubeMonitoringClient            monitoringclient.Interface
   143	        k8sClient                       kubernetes.Interface
   144	        informers                       map[string]*informers.ForResource
   145	        nsInformer                      cache.SharedIndexInformer
   146	        eventInterval                   time.Duration
   147	        stopChannel                     chan struct{}
   148	        configGenerator                 *prometheus.ConfigGenerator
   149	        kubeConfigPath                  string
   150	        podMonitorNamespaceSelector     *metav1.LabelSelector
   151	        serviceMonitorNamespaceSelector *metav1.LabelSelector
   152	        scrapeConfigNamespaceSelector   *metav1.LabelSelector
   153	        probeNamespaceSelector          *metav1.LabelSelector
   154	        resourceSelector                *prometheus.ResourceSelector
   155	        store                           *assets.StoreBuilder
   156	        prometheusCR                    *monitoringv1.Prometheus
   157	}
   158	
   159	func getNamespaceInformer(ctx context.Context, allowList, denyList map[string]struct{}, promOperatorLogger *slog.Logger, clientset kubernetes.Interface, operatorMetrics *operator.Metrics) (cache.SharedIndexInformer, error) {
   160	        kubernetesVersion, err := clientset.Discovery().ServerVersion()
   161	        if err != nil {
   162	                return nil, err
   163	        }
   164	        kubernetesSemverVersion, err := semver.ParseTolerant(kubernetesVersion.String())
   165	        if err != nil {
   166	                return nil, err
   167	        }
   168	        lw, _, err := listwatch.NewNamespaceListWatchFromClient(
   169	                ctx,
   170	                promOperatorLogger,
   171	                kubernetesSemverVersion,
   172	                clientset.CoreV1(),
   173	                clientset.AuthorizationV1().SelfSubjectAccessReviews(),
   174	                allowList,
   175	                denyList,
   176	        )
   177	        if err != nil {
   178	                return nil, err
   179	        }
   180	
   181	        return cache.NewSharedIndexInformer(
   182	                operatorMetrics.NewInstrumentedListerWatcher(lw),
   183	                &v1.Namespace{}, resyncPeriod, cache.Indexers{},
   184	        ), nil
   185	
   186	}
   187	
   188	// getInformers returns a map of informers for the given resources.
   189	func getInformers(factory informers.FactoriesForNamespaces) (map[string]*informers.ForResource, error) {
   190	        serviceMonitorInformers, err := informers.NewInformersForResource(factory, monitoringv1.SchemeGroupVersion.WithResource(monitoringv1.ServiceMonitorName))
   191	        if err != nil {
   192	                return nil, err
   193	        }
   194	
   195	        podMonitorInformers, err := informers.NewInformersForResource(factory, monitoringv1.SchemeGroupVersion.WithResource(monitoringv1.PodMonitorName))
   196	        if err != nil {
   197	                return nil, err
   198	        }
   199	
   200	        probeInformers, err := informers.NewInformersForResource(factory, monitoringv1.SchemeGroupVersion.WithResource(monitoringv1.ProbeName))
   201	        if err != nil {
   202	                return nil, err
   203	        }
   204	
   205	        scrapeConfigInformers, err := informers.NewInformersForResource(factory, promv1alpha1.SchemeGroupVersion.WithResource(promv1alpha1.ScrapeConfigName))
   206	        if err != nil {
   207	                return nil, err
   208	        }
   209	
   210	        return map[string]*informers.ForResource{
   211	                monitoringv1.ServiceMonitorName: serviceMonitorInformers,
   212	                monitoringv1.PodMonitorName:     podMonitorInformers,
   213	                monitoringv1.ProbeName:          probeInformers,
   214	                promv1alpha1.ScrapeConfigName:   scrapeConfigInformers,
   215	        }, nil
   216	}
   217	
   218	// Watch wrapped informers and wait for an initial sync.
   219	func (w *PrometheusCRWatcher) Watch(upstreamEvents chan Event, upstreamErrors chan error) error {
   220	        success := true
   221	        // this channel needs to be buffered because notifications are asynchronous and neither producers nor consumers wait
   222	        notifyEvents := make(chan struct{}, 1)
   223	
   224	        if w.nsInformer != nil {
   225	                go w.nsInformer.Run(w.stopChannel)
   226	                if ok := w.WaitForNamedCacheSync("namespace", w.nsInformer.HasSynced); !ok {
   227	                        success = false
   228	                }
   229	
   230	                _, _ = w.nsInformer.AddEventHandler(cache.ResourceEventHandlerFuncs{
   231	                        UpdateFunc: func(oldObj, newObj interface{}) {
   232	                                old := oldObj.(*v1.Namespace)
   233	                                cur := newObj.(*v1.Namespace)
   234	
   235	                                // Periodic resync may resend the Namespace without changes
   236	                                // in-between.
   237	                                if old.ResourceVersion == cur.ResourceVersion {
   238	                                        return
   239	                                }
   240	
   241	                                for name, selector := range map[string]*metav1.LabelSelector{
   242	                                        "PodMonitorNamespaceSelector":     w.podMonitorNamespaceSelector,
   243	                                        "ServiceMonitorNamespaceSelector": w.serviceMonitorNamespaceSelector,
   244	                                        "ProbeNamespaceSelector":          w.probeNamespaceSelector,
   245	                                        "ScrapeConfigNamespaceSelector":   w.scrapeConfigNamespaceSelector,
   246	                                } {
   247	                                        sync, err := k8sutil.LabelSelectionHasChanged(old.Labels, cur.Labels, selector)
   248	                                        if err != nil {
   249	                                                w.logger.Error("Failed to check label selection between namespaces while handling namespace updates", "selector", name, "error", err)
   250	                                                return
   251	                                        }
   252	
   253	                                        if sync {
   254	                                                select {
   255	                                                case notifyEvents <- struct{}{}:
   256	                                                default:
   257	                                                }
   258	                                                return
   259	                                        }
   260	                                }
   261	                        },
   262	                })
   263	        } else {
   264	                w.logger.Info("Unable to watch namespaces since namespace informer is nil")
   265	        }
   266	
   267	        for name, resource := range w.informers {
   268	                resource.Start(w.stopChannel)
   269	
   270	                if ok := w.WaitForNamedCacheSync(name, resource.HasSynced); !ok {
   271	                        w.logger.Info("skipping informer", "informer", name)
   272	                        continue
   273	                }
   274	
   275	                // only send an event notification if there isn't one already
   276	                resource.AddEventHandler(cache.ResourceEventHandlerFuncs{
   277	                        // these functions only write to the notification channel if it's empty to avoid blocking
   278	                        // if scrape config updates are being rate-limited
   279	                        AddFunc: func(obj interface{}) {
   280	                                select {
   281	                                case notifyEvents <- struct{}{}:
   282	                                default:
   283	                                }
   284	                        },
   285	                        UpdateFunc: func(oldObj, newObj interface{}) {
   286	                                select {
   287	                                case notifyEvents <- struct{}{}:
   288	                                default:
   289	                                }
   290	                        },
   291	                        DeleteFunc: func(obj interface{}) {
   292	                                select {
   293	                                case notifyEvents <- struct{}{}:
   294	                                default:
   295	                                }
   296	                        },
   297	                })
   298	        }
   299	        if !success {
   300	                return fmt.Errorf("failed to sync one of the caches")
   301	        }
   302	
   303	        // limit the rate of outgoing events
   304	        w.rateLimitedEventSender(upstreamEvents, notifyEvents)
   305	
   306	        <-w.stopChannel
   307	        return nil
   308	}
   309	
   310	// rateLimitedEventSender sends events to the upstreamEvents channel whenever it gets a notification on the notifyEvents channel,
   311	// but not more frequently than once per w.eventPeriod.
   312	func (w *PrometheusCRWatcher) rateLimitedEventSender(upstreamEvents chan Event, notifyEvents chan struct{}) {
   313	        ticker := time.NewTicker(w.eventInterval)
   314	        defer ticker.Stop()
   315	
   316	        event := Event{
   317	                Source:  EventSourcePrometheusCR,
   318	                Watcher: Watcher(w),
   319	        }
   320	
   321	        for {
   322	                select {
   323	                case <-w.stopChannel:
   324	                        return
   325	                case <-ticker.C: // throttle events to avoid excessive updates
   326	                        select {
   327	                        case <-notifyEvents:
   328	                                select {
   329	                                case upstreamEvents <- event:
   330	                                default: // put the notification back in the queue if we can't send it upstream
   331	                                        select {
   332	                                        case notifyEvents <- struct{}{}:
   333	                                        default:
   334	                                        }
   335	                                }
   336	                        default:
   337	                        }
   338	                }
   339	        }
   340	}
   341	
   342	func (w *PrometheusCRWatcher) Close() error {
   343	        close(w.stopChannel)
   344	        return nil
   345	}
   346	
   347	func (w *PrometheusCRWatcher) LoadConfig(ctx context.Context) (*promconfig.Config, error) {
   348	        promCfg := &promconfig.Config{}
   349	
   350	        if w.resourceSelector != nil {
   351	                serviceMonitorInstances, err := w.resourceSelector.SelectServiceMonitors(ctx, w.informers[monitoringv1.ServiceMonitorName].ListAllByNamespace)
   352	                if err != nil {
   353	                        return nil, err
   354	                }
   355	
   356	                podMonitorInstances, err := w.resourceSelector.SelectPodMonitors(ctx, w.informers[monitoringv1.PodMonitorName].ListAllByNamespace)
   357	                if err != nil {
   358	                        return nil, err
   359	                }
   360	
   361	                probeInstances, err := w.resourceSelector.SelectProbes(ctx, w.informers[monitoringv1.ProbeName].ListAllByNamespace)
   362	                if err != nil {
   363	                        return nil, err
   364	                }
   365	
   366	                scrapeConfigInstances, err := w.resourceSelector.SelectScrapeConfigs(ctx, w.informers[promv1alpha1.ScrapeConfigName].ListAllByNamespace)
   367	                if err != nil {
   368	                        return nil, err
   369	                }
   370	
   371	                generatedConfig, err := w.configGenerator.GenerateServerConfiguration(
   372	                        w.prometheusCR,
   373	                        serviceMonitorInstances,
   374	                        podMonitorInstances,
   375	                        probeInstances,
   376	                        scrapeConfigInstances,
   377	                        w.store,
   378	                        nil,
   379	                        nil,
   380	                        nil,
   381	                        []string{})
   382	                if err != nil {
   383	                        return nil, err
   384	                }
   385	
   386	                unmarshalErr := yaml.Unmarshal(generatedConfig, promCfg)
   387	                if unmarshalErr != nil {
   388	                        return nil, unmarshalErr
   389	                }
   390	
   391	                // set kubeconfig path to service discovery configs, else kubernetes_sd will always attempt in-cluster
   392	                // authentication even if running with a detected kubeconfig
   393	                for _, scrapeConfig := range promCfg.ScrapeConfigs {
   394	                        for _, serviceDiscoveryConfig := range scrapeConfig.ServiceDiscoveryConfigs {
   395	                                if serviceDiscoveryConfig.Name() == "kubernetes" {
   396	                                        sdConfig := interface{}(serviceDiscoveryConfig).(*kubeDiscovery.SDConfig)
   397	                                        sdConfig.KubeConfig = w.kubeConfigPath
   398	                                }
   399	                        }
   400	                }
   401	                return promCfg, nil
   402	        } else {
   403	                w.logger.Info("Unable to load config since resource selector is nil, returning empty prometheus config")
   404	                return promCfg, nil
   405	        }
   406	}
   407	
   408	// WaitForNamedCacheSync adds a timeout to the informer's wait for the cache to be ready.
   409	// If the PrometheusCRWatcher is unable to load an informer within 15 seconds, the method is
   410	// cancelled and returns false. A successful informer load will return true. This method also
   411	// will be cancelled if the target allocator's stopChannel is called before it returns.
   412	//
   413	// This method is inspired by the upstream prometheus-operator implementation, with a shorter timeout
   414	// and support for the PrometheusCRWatcher's stopChannel.
   415	// https://github.com/prometheus-operator/prometheus-operator/blob/293c16c854ce69d1da9fdc8f0705de2d67bfdbfa/pkg/operator/operator.go#L433
   416	func (w *PrometheusCRWatcher) WaitForNamedCacheSync(controllerName string, inf cache.InformerSynced) bool {
   417	        ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), time.Second*15)
   418	        t := time.NewTicker(time.Second * 5)
   419	        defer t.Stop()
   420	
   421	        go func() {
   422	                for {
   423	                        select {
   424	                        case <-t.C:
   425	                                w.logger.Debug("cache sync not yet completed")
   426	                        case <-ctx.Done():
   427	                                return
   428	                        case <-w.stopChannel:
   429	                                w.logger.Warn("stop received, shutting down cache syncing")
   430	                                cancel()
   431	                                return
   432	                        }
   433	                }
   434	        }()
   435	
   436	        ok := cache.WaitForNamedCacheSync(controllerName, ctx.Done(), inf)
   437	        if !ok {
   438	                w.logger.Error("failed to sync cache")
   439	        } else {
   440	                w.logger.Debug("successfully synced cache")
   441	        }
   442	
   443	        return ok
   444	}
   445

   101	
   102	// StringToModelOrTimeDurationHookFunc returns a DecodeHookFuncType
   103	// that converts string to time.Duration, which can also be used
   104	// as model.Duration.
   105	func StringToModelOrTimeDurationHookFunc() mapstructure.DecodeHookFuncType {
   106	        return func(
   107	                f reflect.Type,
   108	                t reflect.Type,
   109	                data interface{},
   110	        ) (interface{}, error) {
   111	                if f.Kind() != reflect.String {
   112	                        return data, nil
   113	                }
   114	
   115	                if t != reflect.TypeOf(model.Duration(5)) && t != reflect.TypeOf(time.Duration(5)) {
   116	                        return data, nil
   117	                }
   118	
   119	                return time.ParseDuration(data.(string))
   120	        }
   121	}
   122	
   123	// MapToPromConfig returns a DecodeHookFuncType that provides a mechanism
   124	// for decoding promconfig.Config involving its own unmarshal logic.
   125	func MapToPromConfig() mapstructure.DecodeHookFuncType {
   126	        return func(
   127	                f reflect.Type,
   128	                t reflect.Type,
   129	                data interface{},
   130	        ) (interface{}, error) {
   131	                if f.Kind() != reflect.Map {
   132	                        return data, nil
   133	                }
   134	
   135	                if t != reflect.TypeOf(&promconfig.Config{}) {
   136	                        return data, nil
   137	                }
   138	
   139	                dataMap := data.(map[any]any)
   140	                mb, err := yaml.Marshal(dataMap)
   141	                if err != nil {
   142	                        return nil, err
   143	                }
   144	
   145	                pConfig := &promconfig.Config{}
   146	                err = yaml.Unmarshal(mb, pConfig)
   147	                if err != nil {
   148	                        return nil, err
   149	                }
   150	                return pConfig, nil
   151	        }
   152	}
   153	
   154	// MapToLabelSelector returns a DecodeHookFuncType that
   155	// provides a mechanism for decoding both matchLabels and matchExpressions from camelcase to lowercase
   156	// because we use yaml unmarshaling that supports lowercase field names if no `yaml` tag is defined
   157	// and metav1.LabelSelector uses `json` tags.
   158	// If both the camelcase and lowercase version is present, then the camelcase version takes precedence.
   159	func MapToLabelSelector() mapstructure.DecodeHookFuncType {
   160	        return func(
   161	                f reflect.Type,
   162	                t reflect.Type,
   163	                data interface{},
   164	        ) (interface{}, error) {
   165	                if f.Kind() != reflect.Map {
   166	                        return data, nil
   167	                }
   168	
   169	                if t != reflect.TypeOf(&metav1.LabelSelector{}) {
   170	                        return data, nil
   171	                }
   172	
   173	                result := &metav1.LabelSelector{}
   174	                fMap := data.(map[any]any)
   175	                if matchLabels, ok := fMap["matchLabels"]; ok {
   176	                        fMap["matchlabels"] = matchLabels
   177	                        delete(fMap, "matchLabels")
   178	                }
   179	                if matchExpressions, ok := fMap["matchExpressions"]; ok {
   180	                        fMap["matchexpressions"] = matchExpressions
   181	                        delete(fMap, "matchExpressions")
   182	                }
   183	
   184	                b, err := yaml.Marshal(fMap)
   185	                if err != nil {
   186	                        return nil, err
   187	                }
   188	
   189	                err = yaml.Unmarshal(b, result)
   190	                if err != nil {
   191	                        return nil, err
   192	                }
   193	                return result, nil
   194	        }
   195	}
   196	
   197	func LoadFromFile(file string, target *Config) error {
   198	        return unmarshal(target, file)
   199	}
   200	
   201	func LoadFromCLI(target *Config, flagSet *pflag.FlagSet) error {
   202	        var err error
   203	        // set the rest of the config attributes based on command-line flag values
   204	        target.RootLogger = zap.New(zap.UseFlagOptions(&zapCmdLineOpts))
   205	        klog.SetLogger(target.RootLogger)
   206	        ctrl.SetLogger(target.RootLogger)
   207	
   208	        if kubeConfigFilePath, changed, flagErr := getKubeConfigFilePath(flagSet); flagErr != nil {
   209	                return flagErr
   210	        } else if changed {
   211	                target.KubeConfigFilePath = kubeConfigFilePath
   212	        }
   213	        clusterConfig, err := clientcmd.BuildConfigFromFlags("", target.KubeConfigFilePath)
   214	        if err != nil {
   215	                pathError := &fs.PathError{}
   216	                if ok := errors.As(err, &pathError); !ok {
   217	                        return err
   218	                }
   219	                clusterConfig, err = rest.InClusterConfig()
   220	                if err != nil {
   221	                        return err
   222	                }
   223	                target.KubeConfigFilePath = ""
   224	        }
   225	        target.ClusterConfig = clusterConfig
   226	
   227	        if listenAddr, changed, flagErr := getListenAddr(flagSet); flagErr != nil {
   228	                return flagErr
   229	        } else if changed {
   230	                target.ListenAddr = listenAddr
   231	        }
   232	
   233	        if prometheusCREnabled, changed, flagErr := getPrometheusCREnabled(flagSet); flagErr != nil {
   234	                return flagErr
   235	        } else if changed {
   236	                target.PrometheusCR.Enabled = prometheusCREnabled
   237	        }
   238	
   239	        if httpsEnabled, changed, err := getHttpsEnabled(flagSet); err != nil {
   240	                return err
   241	        } else if changed {
   242	                target.HTTPS.Enabled = httpsEnabled
   243	        }
   244	
   245	        if listenAddrHttps, changed, err := getHttpsListenAddr(flagSet); err != nil {
   246	                return err
   247	        } else if changed {
   248	                target.HTTPS.ListenAddr = listenAddrHttps
   249	        }
   250	
   251	        if caFilePath, changed, err := getHttpsCAFilePath(flagSet); err != nil {
   252	                return err
   253	        } else if changed {
   254	                target.HTTPS.CAFilePath = caFilePath
   255	        }
   256	
   257	        if tlsCertFilePath, changed, err := getHttpsTLSCertFilePath(flagSet); err != nil {
   258	                return err
   259	        } else if changed {
   260	                target.HTTPS.TLSCertFilePath = tlsCertFilePath
   261	        }
   262	
   263	        if tlsKeyFilePath, changed, err := getHttpsTLSKeyFilePath(flagSet); err != nil {
   264	                return err
   265	        } else if changed {
   266	                target.HTTPS.TLSKeyFilePath = tlsKeyFilePath
   267	        }
   268	
   269	        return nil
   270	}
   271	
   272	// LoadFromEnv loads configuration from environment variables.
   273	func LoadFromEnv(target *Config) error {
   274	        if ns, ok := os.LookupEnv("OTELCOL_NAMESPACE"); ok {
   275	                target.CollectorNamespace = ns
   276	        }
   277	        return nil
   278	}
   279	
   280	// unmarshal decodes the contents of the configFile into the cfg argument, using a
   281	// mapstructure decoder with the following notable behaviors.
   282	// Decodes time.Duration from strings (see StringToModelDurationHookFunc).
   283	// Allows custom unmarshaling for promconfig.Config struct that implements yaml.Unmarshaler (see MapToPromConfig).
   284	// Allows custom unmarshaling for metav1.LabelSelector struct using both camelcase and lowercase field names (see MapToLabelSelector).
   285	func unmarshal(cfg *Config, configFile string) error {
   286	        yamlFile, err := os.ReadFile(configFile)
   287	        if err != nil {
   288	                return err
   289	        }
   290	
   291	        m := make(map[string]interface{})
   292	        err = yaml.Unmarshal(yamlFile, &m)
   293	        if err != nil {
   294	                return fmt.Errorf("error unmarshaling YAML: %w", err)
   295	        }
   296	
   297	        dc := mapstructure.DecoderConfig{
   298	                TagName: "yaml",
   299	                Result:  cfg,
   300	                DecodeHook: mapstructure.ComposeDecodeHookFunc(
   301	                        StringToModelOrTimeDurationHookFunc(),
   302	                        MapToPromConfig(),
   303	                        MapToLabelSelector(),
   304	                ),
   305	        }
   306	
   307	        decoder, err := mapstructure.NewDecoder(&dc)
   308	        if err != nil {
   309	                return err
   310	        }
   311	        if err := decoder.Decode(m); err != nil {
   312	                return err
   313	        }
   314	
   315	        return nil
   316	}
   317	
   318	func CreateDefaultConfig() Config {
   319	        return Config{
   320	                ListenAddr:         DefaultListenAddr,
   321	                KubeConfigFilePath: DefaultKubeConfigFilePath,
   322	                HTTPS: HTTPSServerConfig{
   323	                        ListenAddr: DefaultHttpsListenAddr,
   324	                },
   325	                AllocationStrategy:         DefaultAllocationStrategy,
   326	                AllocationFallbackStrategy: "",
   327	                FilterStrategy:             DefaultFilterStrategy,
   328	                PrometheusCR: PrometheusCRConfig{
   329	                        ScrapeInterval:                  DefaultCRScrapeInterval,
   330	                        ServiceMonitorNamespaceSelector: &metav1.LabelSelector{},
   331	                        PodMonitorNamespaceSelector:     &metav1.LabelSelector{},
   332	                        ScrapeConfigNamespaceSelector:   &metav1.LabelSelector{},
   333	                        ProbeNamespaceSelector:          &metav1.LabelSelector{},
   334	                        ScrapeProtocols:                 defaultScrapeProtocolsCR,
   335	                },
   336	                CollectorNotReadyGracePeriod: DefaultCollectorNotReadyGracePeriod,
   337	        }
   338	}
   339	
   340	func Load(args []string) (*Config, error) {
   341	        var err error
   342	
   343	        flagSet := getFlagSet(pflag.ExitOnError)
   344	        err = flagSet.Parse(args)
   345	        if err != nil {
   346	                return nil, err
   347	        }
   348	
   349	        config := CreateDefaultConfig()
   350	
   351	        // load the config from the config file
   352	        configFilePath, err := getConfigFilePath(flagSet)
   353	        if err != nil {
   354	                return nil, err
   355	        }
   356	        err = LoadFromFile(configFilePath, &config)
   357	        if err != nil {
   358	                return nil, err
   359	        }
   360	
   361	        err = LoadFromEnv(&config)
   362	        if err != nil {
   363	                return nil, err
   364	        }
   365	
   366	        err = LoadFromCLI(&config, flagSet)
   367	        if err != nil {
   368	                return nil, err
   369	        }
   370	
   371	        return &config, nil
   372	}
   373	
   374	// ValidateConfig validates the cli and file configs together.
   375	func ValidateConfig(config *Config) error {
   376	        scrapeConfigsPresent := (config.PromConfig != nil && len(config.PromConfig.ScrapeConfigs) > 0)
   377	        if !(config.PrometheusCR.Enabled || scrapeConfigsPresent) {
   378	                return fmt.Errorf("at least one scrape config must be defined, or Prometheus CR watching must be enabled")
   379	        }
   380	        if config.CollectorNamespace == "" {
   381	                return fmt.Errorf("collector namespace must be set")
   382	        }
   383	        if len(config.PrometheusCR.AllowNamespaces) != 0 && len(config.PrometheusCR.DenyNamespaces) != 0 {
   384	                return fmt.Errorf("only one of allowNamespaces or denyNamespaces can be set")
   385	        }
   386	        return nil
   387	}
   388	
   389	func (c HTTPSServerConfig) NewTLSConfig() (*tls.Config, error) {
   390	        cert, err := tls.LoadX509KeyPair(c.TLSCertFilePath, c.TLSKeyFilePath)
   391	        if err != nil {
   392	                return nil, err
   393	        }
   394	
   395	        caCert, err := os.ReadFile(c.CAFilePath)
   396	        if err != nil {
   397	                return nil, err
   398	        }
   399	
   400	        caCertPool := x509.NewCertPool()
   401	        caCertPool.AppendCertsFromPEM(caCert)
   402	
   403	        tlsConfig := &tls.Config{
   404	                Certificates: []tls.Certificate{cert},
   405	                ClientAuth:   tls.RequireAndVerifyClientCert,
   406	                ClientCAs:    caCertPool,
   407	                MinVersion:   tls.VersionTLS12,
   408	        }
   409	        return tlsConfig, nil
   410	}
   411	
   412	// GetAllowDenyLists returns the allow and deny lists as maps. If the allow list is empty, it defaults to all namespaces.
   413	// If the deny list is empty, it defaults to an empty map.
   414	func (c PrometheusCRConfig) GetAllowDenyLists() (map[string]struct{}, map[string]struct{}) {
   415	        allowList := map[string]struct{}{}
   416	        if len(c.AllowNamespaces) != 0 {
   417	                for _, ns := range c.AllowNamespaces {
   418	                        allowList[ns] = struct{}{}
   419	                }
   420	        } else {
   421	                allowList = map[string]struct{}{v1.NamespaceAll: {}}
   422	        }
   423	
   424	        denyList := map[string]struct{}{}
   425	        if len(c.DenyNamespaces) != 0 {
   426	                for _, ns := range c.DenyNamespaces {
   427	                        denyList[ns] = struct{}{}
   428	                }
   429	        }
   430	
   431	        return allowList, denyList
   432	}

   137	                }
   138	                // apply the initial configuration
   139	                promConfig, loadErr := promWatcher.LoadConfig(ctx)
   140	                if loadErr != nil {
   141	                        setupLog.Error(loadErr, "Can't load initial Prometheus configuration from Prometheus CRs")
   142	                        os.Exit(1)
   143	                }
   144	                loadErr = targetDiscoverer.ApplyConfig(allocatorWatcher.EventSourcePrometheusCR, promConfig.ScrapeConfigs)
   145	                if loadErr != nil {
   146	                        setupLog.Error(loadErr, "Can't load initial scrape targets from Prometheus CRs")
   147	                        os.Exit(1)
   148	                }
   149	                runGroup.Add(
   150	                        func() error {
   151	                                promWatcherErr := promWatcher.Watch(eventChan, errChan)
   152	                                setupLog.Info("Prometheus watcher exited")
   153	                                return promWatcherErr
   154	                        },
   155	                        func(_ error) {
   156	                                setupLog.Info("Closing prometheus watcher")
   157	                                promWatcherErr := promWatcher.Close()
   158	                                if promWatcherErr != nil {
   159	                                        setupLog.Error(promWatcherErr, "prometheus watcher failed to close")
   160	                                }
   161	                        })
   162	        }
   163	        runGroup.Add(
   164	                func() error {
   165	                        discoveryManagerErr := discoveryManager.Run()
   166	                        setupLog.Info("Discovery manager exited")
   167	                        return discoveryManagerErr
   168	                },
   169	                func(_ error) {
   170	                        setupLog.Info("Closing discovery manager")
   171	                        discoveryCancel()
   172	                })
   173	        runGroup.Add(
   174	                func() error {
   175	                        // Initial loading of the config file's scrape config
   176	                        if cfg.PromConfig != nil && len(cfg.PromConfig.ScrapeConfigs) > 0 {
   177	                                applyErr := targetDiscoverer.ApplyConfig(allocatorWatcher.EventSourceConfigMap, cfg.PromConfig.ScrapeConfigs)
   178	                                if applyErr != nil {
   179	                                        setupLog.Error(err, "Unable to apply initial configuration")
   180	                                        return err
   181	                                }
   182	                        } else {
   183	                                setupLog.Info("Prometheus config empty, skipping initial discovery configuration")
   184	                        }
   185	
   186	                        tErr := targetDiscoverer.Run()
   187	                        setupLog.Info("Target discoverer exited")
   188	                        return tErr
   189	                },
   190	                func(_ error) {
   191	                        setupLog.Info("Closing target discoverer")
   192	                        targetDiscoverer.Close()
   193	                })
   194	        runGroup.Add(
   195	                func() error {
   196	                        watchErr := collectorWatcher.Watch(cfg.CollectorNamespace, cfg.CollectorSelector, allocator.SetCollectors)
   197	                        setupLog.Info("Collector watcher exited")
   198	                        return watchErr
   199	                },
   200	                func(_ error) {
   201	                        setupLog.Info("Closing collector watcher")
   202	                        collectorWatcher.Close()
   203	                })
   204	        runGroup.Add(
   205	                func() error {
   206	                        startErr := srv.Start()
   207	                        setupLog.Info("Server failed to start")
   208	                        return startErr
   209	                },
   210	                func(_ error) {
   211	                        setupLog.Info("Closing server")
   212	                        if shutdownErr := srv.Shutdown(ctx); shutdownErr != nil {
   213	                                setupLog.Error(shutdownErr, "Error on server shutdown")
   214	                        }
   215	                })
   216	        if cfg.HTTPS.Enabled {
   217	                runGroup.Add(
   218	                        func() error {
   219	                                startErr := srv.StartHTTPS()
   220	                                setupLog.Info("HTTPS Server failed to start")
   221	                                return startErr
   222	                        },
   223	                        func(_ error) {
   224	                                setupLog.Info("Closing HTTPS server")
   225	                                if shutdownErr := srv.ShutdownHTTPS(ctx); shutdownErr != nil {
   226	                                        setupLog.Error(shutdownErr, "Error on HTTPS server shutdown")
   227	                                }
   228	                        })
   229	        }
   230	        meter := otel.GetMeterProvider().Meter("targetallocator")
   231	        eventsMetric, err := meter.Int64Counter("opentelemetry_allocator_events", metric.WithDescription("Number of events in the channel."))
   232	        if err != nil {
   233	                panic(err)
   234	        }
   235	        runGroup.Add(
   236	                func() error {
   237	                        for {
   238	                                select {
   239	                                case event := <-eventChan:
   240	                                        eventsMetric.Add(context.Background(), 1, metric.WithAttributes(attribute.String("source", event.Source.String())))
   241	                                        loadConfig, err := event.Watcher.LoadConfig(ctx)
   242	                                        if err != nil {
   243	                                                setupLog.Error(err, "Unable to load configuration")
   244	                                                continue
   245	                                        }
   246	                                        err = targetDiscoverer.ApplyConfig(event.Source, loadConfig.ScrapeConfigs)
   247	                                        if err != nil {
   248	                                                setupLog.Error(err, "Unable to apply configuration")
   249	                                                continue
   250	                                        }
   251	                                case err := <-errChan:
   252	                                        setupLog.Error(err, "Watcher error")
   253	                                case <-eventCloser:
   254	                                        return nil
   255	                                }
   256	                        }
   257	                },
   258	                func(_ error) {
   259	                        setupLog.Info("Closing watcher loop")
   260	                        close(eventCloser)
   261	                })
   262	        runGroup.Add(
   263	                func() error {
   264	                        for {
   265	                                select {
   266	                                case <-interrupts:
   267	                                        setupLog.Info("Received interrupt")
   268	                                        return nil
   269	                                case <-eventCloser:
   270	                                        return nil
   271	                                }
   272	                        }
   273	                },
   274	                func(_ error) {
   275	                        setupLog.Info("Closing interrupt loop")
   276	                })
   277	        if runErr := runGroup.Run(); runErr != nil {
   278	                setupLog.Error(runErr, "run group exited")
   279	        }
   280	        setupLog.Info("Target allocator exited.")
   281	}
   282

     4	// Package autodetect is for auto-detecting traits from the environment (platform, APIs, ...).
     5	package autodetect

     9	        "fmt"
    10	        "slices"

    29	var _ AutoDetect = (*autoDetect)(nil)

    31	// AutoDetect provides an assortment of routines that auto-detect traits based on the runtime.
    32	type AutoDetect interface {
    33	        OpenShiftRoutesAvailability() (openshift.RoutesAvailability, error)
    34	        PrometheusCRsAvailability() (prometheus.Availability, error)
    35	        RBACPermissions(ctx context.Context) (autoRBAC.Availability, error)
    36	        CertManagerAvailability(ctx context.Context) (certmanager.Availability, error)
    37	        TargetAllocatorAvailability() (targetallocator.Availability, error)
    38	        CollectorAvailability() (collector.Availability, error)
    39	        OpAmpBridgeAvailablity() (opampbridge.Availability, error)
    40	        FIPSEnabled(ctx context.Context) bool
    41	}
    42	
    43	type autoDetect struct {
    44	        dcl      discovery.DiscoveryInterface
    45	        reviewer *rbac.Reviewer
    46	}
    47	
    48	// New creates a new auto-detection worker, using the given client when talking to the current cluster.
    49	func New(restConfig *rest.Config, reviewer *rbac.Reviewer) (AutoDetect, error) {
    50	        dcl, err := discovery.NewDiscoveryClientForConfig(restConfig)
    51	        if err != nil {
    52	                // it's pretty much impossible to get into this problem, as most of the
    53	                // code branches from the previous call just won't fail at all,
    54	                // but let's handle this error anyway...
    55	                return nil, err
    56	        }
    57	
    58	        return &autoDetect{
    59	                dcl:      dcl,
    60	                reviewer: reviewer,
    61	        }, nil
    62	}
    63	
    64	// PrometheusCRsAvailability checks if Prometheus CRDs are available.
    65	func (a *autoDetect) PrometheusCRsAvailability() (prometheus.Availability, error) {
    66	        apiList, err := a.dcl.ServerGroups()
    67	        if err != nil {
    68	                return prometheus.NotAvailable, err
    69	        }
    70	
    71	        foundServiceMonitor := false
    72	        foundPodMonitor := false
    73	        apiGroups := apiList.Groups
    74	        for i := 0; i < len(apiGroups); i++ {
    75	                if apiGroups[i].Name == "monitoring.coreos.com" {
    76	                        for _, version := range apiGroups[i].Versions {
    77	                                resources, err := a.dcl.ServerResourcesForGroupVersion(version.GroupVersion)
    78	                                if err != nil {
    79	                                        return prometheus.NotAvailable, err
    80	                                }
    81	
    82	                                for _, resource := range resources.APIResources {
    83	                                        if resource.Kind == "ServiceMonitor" {
    84	                                                foundServiceMonitor = true
    85	                                        } else if resource.Kind == "PodMonitor" {
    86	                                                foundPodMonitor = true
    87	                                        }
    88	                                }
    89	                        }
    90	                }
    91	        }
    92	
    93	        if foundServiceMonitor && foundPodMonitor {
    94	                return prometheus.Available, nil
    95	        }
    96	
    97	        return prometheus.NotAvailable, nil
    98	}
    99	
   100	// OpenShiftRoutesAvailability checks if OpenShift Route are available.
   101	func (a *autoDetect) OpenShiftRoutesAvailability() (openshift.RoutesAvailability, error) {
   102	        apiList, err := a.dcl.ServerGroups()
   103	        if err != nil {
   104	                return openshift.RoutesNotAvailable, err
   105	        }
   106	
   107	        apiGroups := apiList.Groups
   108	        for i := 0; i < len(apiGroups); i++ {
   109	                if apiGroups[i].Name == "route.openshift.io" {
   110	                        return openshift.RoutesAvailable, nil
   111	                }
   112	        }
   113	
   114	        return openshift.RoutesNotAvailable, nil
   115	}
   116	
   117	func (a *autoDetect) RBACPermissions(ctx context.Context) (autoRBAC.Availability, error) {
   118	        w, err := autoRBAC.CheckRBACPermissions(ctx, a.reviewer)
   119	        if err != nil {
   120	                return autoRBAC.NotAvailable, err
   121	        }
   122	        if w != nil {
   123	                return autoRBAC.NotAvailable, fmt.Errorf("missing permissions: %s", w)
   124	        }
   125	
   126	        return autoRBAC.Available, nil
   127	}
   128	
   129	func (a *autoDetect) CertManagerAvailability(ctx context.Context) (certmanager.Availability, error) {
   130	        apiList, err := a.dcl.ServerGroups()
   131	        if err != nil {
   132	                return certmanager.NotAvailable, err
   133	        }
   134	
   135	        apiGroups := apiList.Groups
   136	        certManagerFound := false
   137	        for i := 0; i < len(apiGroups); i++ {
   138	                if apiGroups[i].Name == "cert-manager.io" {
   139	                        certManagerFound = true
   140	                        break
   141	                }
   142	        }
   143	
   144	        if !certManagerFound {
   145	                return certmanager.NotAvailable, nil
   146	        }
   147	
   148	        w, err := certmanager.CheckCertManagerPermissions(ctx, a.reviewer)
   149	        if err != nil {
   150	                return certmanager.NotAvailable, err
   151	        }
   152	        if w != nil {
   153	                return certmanager.NotAvailable, fmt.Errorf("missing permissions: %s", w)
   154	        }
   155	
   156	        return certmanager.Available, nil
   157	}
   158	
   159	// TargetAllocatorAvailability checks if TargetAllocator CR are available.
   160	func (a *autoDetect) TargetAllocatorAvailability() (targetallocator.Availability, error) {
   161	        apiList, err := a.dcl.ServerGroups()
   162	        if err != nil {
   163	                return targetallocator.NotAvailable, err
   164	        }
   165	
   166	        apiGroups := apiList.Groups
   167	        otelGroupIndex := slices.IndexFunc(apiGroups, func(group metav1.APIGroup) bool {
   168	                return group.Name == "opentelemetry.io"
   169	        })
   170	        if otelGroupIndex == -1 {
   171	                return targetallocator.NotAvailable, nil
   172	        }
   173	
   174	        otelGroup := apiGroups[otelGroupIndex]
   175	        for _, groupVersion := range otelGroup.Versions {
   176	                resourceList, err := a.dcl.ServerResourcesForGroupVersion(groupVersion.GroupVersion)
   177	                if err != nil {
   178	                        return targetallocator.NotAvailable, err
   179	                }
   180	                targetAllocatorIndex := slices.IndexFunc(resourceList.APIResources, func(group metav1.APIResource) bool {
   181	                        return group.Kind == "TargetAllocator"
   182	                })
   183	                if targetAllocatorIndex >= 0 {
   184	                        return targetallocator.Available, nil
   185	                }
   186	        }
   187	
   188	        return targetallocator.NotAvailable, nil
   189	}
   190

   259	// ApplyAutoDetect attempts to automatically detect relevant information for this operator.
   260	func ApplyAutoDetect(autoDetect AutoDetect, c *config.Config, logger logr.Logger) error {
   261	        logger.V(2).Info("auto-detecting the configuration based on the environment")
   262	
   263	        ora, err := autoDetect.OpenShiftRoutesAvailability()
   264	        if err != nil {
   265	                return err
   266	        }
   267	        c.OpenShiftRoutesAvailability = ora
   268	        logger.V(2).Info("openshift routes detected", "availability", ora)
   269	
   270	        pcrd, err := autoDetect.PrometheusCRsAvailability()
   271	        if err != nil {
   272	                return err
   273	        }
   274	        c.PrometheusCRAvailability = pcrd
   275	        logger.V(2).Info("prometheus cr detected", "availability", pcrd)
   276	
   277	        rAuto, err := autoDetect.RBACPermissions(context.Background())
   278	        if err != nil {
   279	                logger.V(2).Info("the rbac permissions are not set for the operator", "reason", err)
   280	        }
   281	        c.CreateRBACPermissions = rAuto
   282	        logger.V(2).Info("create rbac permissions detected", "availability", rAuto)
   283	
   284	        cmAvl, err := autoDetect.CertManagerAvailability(context.Background())
   285	        if err != nil {
   286	                logger.V(2).Info("the cert manager crd and permissions are not set for the operator", "reason", err)
   287	        }
   288	        c.CertManagerAvailability = cmAvl
   289	        logger.V(2).Info("the cert manager crd and permissions are set for the operator", "availability", cmAvl)
   290	
   291	        taAvl, err := autoDetect.TargetAllocatorAvailability()
   292	        if err != nil {
   293	                return err
   294	        }
   295	        c.TargetAllocatorAvailability = taAvl
   296	        logger.V(2).Info("determined TargetAllocator CRD availability", "availability", cmAvl)
   297	
   298	        coAvl, err := autoDetect.CollectorAvailability()
   299	        if err != nil {
   300	                return err
   301	        }
   302	        c.CollectorAvailability = coAvl
   303	        logger.V(2).Info("determined Collector CRD availability", "availability", coAvl)
   304	
   305	        opAvl, err := autoDetect.OpAmpBridgeAvailablity()
   306	        if err != nil {
   307	                return err
   308	        }
   309	        c.OpAmpBridgeAvailability = opAvl
   310	        logger.V(2).Info("determined OpAmpBridge CRD availability", "availability", coAvl)
   311	
   312	        return nil
   313	}

Now I need to understand the solution. The problem is clear:

1. In `getInformers()` function (lines 188-216 of promOperator.go), all four CRD types are always queried
2. There's no check if the CRDs exist before creating informers
3. Even if selectors are nil, informers are still created

The solution should be:
1. Check if each CRD exists in the cluster before creating its informer
2. Only create informers for CRDs that actually exist
3. Log a warning if a CRD is not available

Let me create a function to check CRD availability similar to the autodetect pattern. First, let me write a test script to understand the issue better:

🎬 ACTION

"""
Test script to verify the issue with CRD checking.

The issue is that target-allocator tries to watch all CRDs (ServiceMonitor, PodMonitor, Probe, ScrapeConfig)
regardless of whether they exist in the cluster or not.
"""

import subprocess
import sys

def main():
    print("Checking the problematic code in promOperator.go...")
    
    # Check that getInformers function exists
    result = subprocess.run(
        ["grep", "-n", "func getInformers", "/testbed/cmd/otel-allocator/internal/watcher/promOperator.go"],
        capture_output=True,
        text=True
    )
    
    if result.returncode != 0:
        print("ERROR: Could not find getInformers function")
        return 1
    
    print(f"Found getInformers function at: {result.stdout.strip()}")
    
    # Check that it creates informers for all 4 CRD types
    result = subprocess.run(
        ["grep", "-A", "30", "func getInformers", "/testbed/cmd/otel-allocator/internal/watcher/promOperator.go"],
        capture_output=True,
        text=True
    )
    
    crds = ["ServiceMonitor", "PodMonitor", "Probe", "ScrapeConfig"]
    for crd in crds:
        if crd in result.stdout:
            print(f"✓ Found {crd} informer creation (unconditional)")
        else:
            print(f"✗ Did not find {crd} informer creation")
    
    # Check if there'"'"'s any CRD existence check
    result = subprocess.run(
        ["grep", "-i", "crd.*exist\|exist.*crd\|server.*resource\|discovery", "/testbed/cmd/otel-allocator/internal/watcher/promOperator.go"],
        capture_output=True,
        text=True
    )
    
    if result.returncode != 0 or not result.stdout.strip():
        print("\n✗ No CRD existence check found in promOperator.go")
    else:
        print(f"\n✓ Found potential CRD check: {result.stdout.strip()}")
    
    print("\nISSUE CONFIRMED: All CRD informers are created unconditionally!")
    print("This causes errors when CRDs don'"'"'t exist in the cluster.")
    return 0

if __name__ == "__main__":
    sys.exit(main())

// getInformers returns a map of informers for the given resources.
func getInformers(factory informers.FactoriesForNamespaces) (map[string]*informers.ForResource, error) {
        serviceMonitorInformers, err := informers.NewInformersForResource(factory, monitoringv1.SchemeGroupVersion.WithResource(monitoringv1.ServiceMonitorName))
        if err != nil {
                return nil, err
        }

        podMonitorInformers, err := informers.NewInformersForResource(factory, monitoringv1.SchemeGroupVersion.WithResource(monitoringv1.PodMonitorName))
        if err != nil {
                return nil, err
        }

        probeInformers, err := informers.NewInformersForResource(factory, monitoringv1.SchemeGroupVersion.WithResource(monitoringv1.ProbeName))
        if err != nil {
                return nil, err
        }

        scrapeConfigInformers, err := informers.NewInformersForResource(factory, promv1alpha1.SchemeGroupVersion.WithResource(promv1alpha1.ScrapeConfigName))
        if err != nil {
                return nil, err
        }

        return map[string]*informers.ForResource{
                monitoringv1.ServiceMonitorName: serviceMonitorInformers,
                monitoringv1.PodMonitorName:     podMonitorInformers,
                monitoringv1.ProbeName:          probeInformers,
                promv1alpha1.ScrapeConfigName:   scrapeConfigInformers,
        }, nil
}' --new_str '}

// checkCRDAvailability checks if a specific CRD is available in the cluster.
func checkCRDAvailability(ctx context.Context, client kubernetes.Interface, gvr schema.GroupVersionResource) (bool, error) {
        discoveryClient := client.Discovery()
        
        apiResourceList, err := discoveryClient.ServerResourcesForGroupVersion(gvr.GroupVersion().String())
        if err != nil {
                // If we get a NotFound error, the API group version doesn'"'"'t exist
                return false, nil
        }

        for _, resource := range apiResourceList.APIResources {
                if resource.Name == gvr.Resource {
                        return true, nil
                }
        }

        return false, nil
}

// getInformers returns a map of informers for the given resources.
// It only creates informers for CRDs that exist in the cluster.
func getInformers(ctx context.Context, logger logr.Logger, client kubernetes.Interface, factory informers.FactoriesForNamespaces) (map[string]*informers.ForResource, error) {
        result := make(map[string]*informers.ForResource)

        // Check and create ServiceMonitor informer
        serviceMonitorGVR := monitoringv1.SchemeGroupVersion.WithResource(monitoringv1.ServiceMonitorName)
        serviceMonitorAvailable, err := checkCRDAvailability(ctx, client, serviceMonitorGVR)
        if err != nil {
                logger.Error(err, "Failed to check ServiceMonitor CRD availability")
                return nil, err
        }
        if serviceMonitorAvailable {
                serviceMonitorInformers, err := informers.NewInformersForResource(factory, serviceMonitorGVR)
                if err != nil {
                        return nil, err
                }
                result[monitoringv1.ServiceMonitorName] = serviceMonitorInformers
                logger.Info("ServiceMonitor CRD is available, informer created")
        } else {
                logger.Info("ServiceMonitor CRD is not available, skipping informer creation")
        }

        // Check and create PodMonitor informer
        podMonitorGVR := monitoringv1.SchemeGroupVersion.WithResource(monitoringv1.PodMonitorName)
        podMonitorAvailable, err := checkCRDAvailability(ctx, client, podMonitorGVR)
        if err != nil {
                logger.Error(err, "Failed to check PodMonitor CRD availability")
                return nil, err
        }
        if podMonitorAvailable {
                podMonitorInformers, err := informers.NewInformersForResource(factory, podMonitorGVR)
                if err != nil {
                        return nil, err
                }
                result[monitoringv1.PodMonitorName] = podMonitorInformers
                logger.Info("PodMonitor CRD is available, informer created")
        } else {
                logger.Info("PodMonitor CRD is not available, skipping informer creation")
        }

        // Check and create Probe informer
        probeGVR := monitoringv1.SchemeGroupVersion.WithResource(monitoringv1.ProbeName)
        probeAvailable, err := checkCRDAvailability(ctx, client, probeGVR)
        if err != nil {
                logger.Error(err, "Failed to check Probe CRD availability")
                return nil, err
        }
        if probeAvailable {
                probeInformers, err := informers.NewInformersForResource(factory, probeGVR)
                if err != nil {
                        return nil, err
                }
                result[monitoringv1.ProbeName] = probeInformers
                logger.Info("Probe CRD is available, informer created")
        } else {
                logger.Info("Probe CRD is not available, skipping informer creation")
        }

        // Check and create ScrapeConfig informer
        scrapeConfigGVR := promv1alpha1.SchemeGroupVersion.WithResource(promv1alpha1.ScrapeConfigName)
        scrapeConfigAvailable, err := checkCRDAvailability(ctx, client, scrapeConfigGVR)
        if err != nil {
                logger.Error(err, "Failed to check ScrapeConfig CRD availability")
                return nil, err
        }
        if scrapeConfigAvailable {
                scrapeConfigInformers, err := informers.NewInformersForResource(factory, scrapeConfigGVR)
                if err != nil {
                        return nil, err
                }
                result[promv1alpha1.ScrapeConfigName] = scrapeConfigInformers
                logger.Info("ScrapeConfig CRD is available, informer created")
        } else {
                logger.Info("ScrapeConfig CRD is not available, skipping informer creation")
        }

        return result, nil
}'

   421	                serviceMonitorInstances, err := w.resourceSelector.SelectServiceMonitors(ctx, w.informers[monitoringv1.ServiceMonitorName].ListAllByNamespace)

   458	                        return nil, unmarshalErr

   470	                }

        }' --new_str 'func (w *PrometheusCRWatcher) LoadConfig(ctx context.Context) (*promconfig.Config, error) {
        promCfg := &promconfig.Config{}

        if w.resourceSelector != nil {
                var serviceMonitorInstances map[string]*monitoringv1.ServiceMonitor
                var podMonitorInstances map[string]*monitoringv1.PodMonitor
                var probeInstances map[string]*monitoringv1.Probe
                var scrapeConfigInstances map[string]*promv1alpha1.ScrapeConfig
                var err error

                // Only select ServiceMonitors if the informer exists
                if w.informers[monitoringv1.ServiceMonitorName] != nil {
                        serviceMonitorInstances, err = w.resourceSelector.SelectServiceMonitors(ctx, w.informers[monitoringv1.ServiceMonitorName].ListAllByNamespace)
                        if err != nil {
                                return nil, err
                        }
                } else {
                        serviceMonitorInstances = make(map[string]*monitoringv1.ServiceMonitor)
                }

                // Only select PodMonitors if the informer exists
                if w.informers[monitoringv1.PodMonitorName] != nil {
                        podMonitorInstances, err = w.resourceSelector.SelectPodMonitors(ctx, w.informers[monitoringv1.PodMonitorName].ListAllByNamespace)
                        if err != nil {
                                return nil, err
                        }
                } else {
                        podMonitorInstances = make(map[string]*monitoringv1.PodMonitor)
                }

                // Only select Probes if the informer exists
                if w.informers[monitoringv1.ProbeName] != nil {
                        probeInstances, err = w.resourceSelector.SelectProbes(ctx, w.informers[monitoringv1.ProbeName].ListAllByNamespace)
                        if err != nil {
                                return nil, err
                        }
                } else {
                        probeInstances = make(map[string]*monitoringv1.Probe)
                }

                // Only select ScrapeConfigs if the informer exists
                if w.informers[promv1alpha1.ScrapeConfigName] != nil {
                        scrapeConfigInstances, err = w.resourceSelector.SelectScrapeConfigs(ctx, w.informers[promv1alpha1.ScrapeConfigName].ListAllByNamespace)
                        if err != nil {
                                return nil, err
                        }
                } else {
                        scrapeConfigInstances = make(map[string]*promv1alpha1.ScrapeConfig)
                }

                generatedConfig, err := w.configGenerator.GenerateServerConfiguration(
                        w.prometheusCR,
                        serviceMonitorInstances,
                        podMonitorInstances,
                        probeInstances,
                        scrapeConfigInstances,
                        w.store,
                        nil,
                        nil,
                        nil,
                        []string{})
                if err != nil {
                        return nil, err
                }

                unmarshalErr := yaml.Unmarshal(generatedConfig, promCfg)
                if unmarshalErr != nil {
                        return nil, unmarshalErr
                }

                // set kubeconfig path to service discovery configs, else kubernetes_sd will always attempt in-cluster
                // authentication even if running with a detected kubeconfig
                for _, scrapeConfig := range promCfg.ScrapeConfigs {
                        for _, serviceDiscoveryConfig := range scrapeConfig.ServiceDiscoveryConfigs {
                                if serviceDiscoveryConfig.Name() == "kubernetes" {
                                        sdConfig := interface{}(serviceDiscoveryConfig).(*kubeDiscovery.SDConfig)
                                        sdConfig.KubeConfig = w.kubeConfigPath
                                }
                        }
                }
                return promCfg, nil
        } else {
                w.logger.Info("Unable to load config since resource selector is nil, returning empty prometheus config")
                return promCfg, nil
        }'

func getTestPrometheusCRWatcher(
	t *testing.T,
	namespace string,
	svcMonitors []*monitoringv1.ServiceMonitor,
	podMonitors []*monitoringv1.PodMonitor,
	probes []*monitoringv1.Probe,
	scrapeConfigs []*promv1alpha1.ScrapeConfig,
	cfg allocatorconfig.Config,
) (*PrometheusCRWatcher, *fcache.FakeControllerSource) {
	mClient := fakemonitoringclient.NewSimpleClientset()
	for _, sm := range svcMonitors {
		if sm != nil {
			_, err := mClient.MonitoringV1().ServiceMonitors(sm.Namespace).Create(context.Background(), sm, metav1.CreateOptions{})
			if err != nil {
				t.Fatal(t, err)
			}
		}
	}
	for _, pm := range podMonitors {
		if pm != nil {
			_, err := mClient.MonitoringV1().PodMonitors(pm.Namespace).Create(context.Background(), pm, metav1.CreateOptions{})
			if err != nil {
				t.Fatal(t, err)
			}
		}
	}
	for _, prb := range probes {
		if prb != nil {
			_, err := mClient.MonitoringV1().Probes(prb.Namespace).Create(context.Background(), prb, metav1.CreateOptions{})
			if err != nil {
				t.Fatal(t, err)
			}
		}
	}

	for _, scc := range scrapeConfigs {
		if scc != nil {
			_, err := mClient.MonitoringV1alpha1().ScrapeConfigs(scc.Namespace).Create(context.Background(), scc, metav1.CreateOptions{})
			if err != nil {
				t.Fatal(t, err)
			}
		}
	}

	k8sClient := fake.NewSimpleClientset()
	_, err := k8sClient.CoreV1().Secrets("test").Create(context.Background(), &v1.Secret{
		ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
			Name:      "basic-auth",
			Namespace: "test",
		},
		Data: map[string][]byte{"username": []byte("admin"), "password": []byte("password")},
	}, metav1.CreateOptions{})
	if err != nil {
		t.Fatal(t, err)
	}
	_, err = k8sClient.CoreV1().Secrets("test").Create(context.Background(), &v1.Secret{
		ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
			Name:      "bearer",
			Namespace: "test",
		},
		Data: map[string][]byte{"token": []byte("bearer-token")},
	}, metav1.CreateOptions{})
	if err != nil {
		t.Fatal(t, err)
	}

	factory := informers.NewMonitoringInformerFactories(map[string]struct{}{v1.NamespaceAll: {}}, map[string]struct{}{}, mClient, 0, nil)
	informers, err := getInformers(factory)
	if err != nil {
		t.Fatal(t, err)
	}

	serviceDiscoveryRole := monitoringv1.ServiceDiscoveryRole("EndpointSlice")

	prom := &monitoringv1.Prometheus{
		ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
			Namespace: namespace,
		},
		Spec: monitoringv1.PrometheusSpec{
			CommonPrometheusFields: monitoringv1.CommonPrometheusFields{
				ScrapeInterval:                  monitoringv1.Duration("30s"),
				ServiceMonitorSelector:          cfg.PrometheusCR.ServiceMonitorSelector,
				PodMonitorSelector:              cfg.PrometheusCR.PodMonitorSelector,
				ServiceMonitorNamespaceSelector: cfg.PrometheusCR.ServiceMonitorNamespaceSelector,
				PodMonitorNamespaceSelector:     cfg.PrometheusCR.PodMonitorNamespaceSelector,
				ProbeSelector:                   cfg.PrometheusCR.ProbeSelector,
				ProbeNamespaceSelector:          cfg.PrometheusCR.ProbeNamespaceSelector,
				ScrapeConfigSelector:            cfg.PrometheusCR.ScrapeConfigSelector,
				ScrapeConfigNamespaceSelector:   cfg.PrometheusCR.ScrapeConfigNamespaceSelector,
				ServiceDiscoveryRole:            &serviceDiscoveryRole,
				Version:                         "2.55.1",
			},
			EvaluationInterval: monitoringv1.Duration("30s"),
		},
	}

	promOperatorLogger := slog.New(slog.NewTextHandler(os.Stderr, &slog.HandlerOptions{Level: slog.LevelWarn}))

	generator, err := prometheus.NewConfigGenerator(promOperatorLogger, prom, prometheus.WithEndpointSliceSupport(), prometheus.WithInlineTLSConfig())
	if err != nil {
		t.Fatal(t, err)
	}

	store := assets.NewStoreBuilder(k8sClient.CoreV1(), k8sClient.CoreV1())
	promRegisterer := prometheusgoclient.NewRegistry()
	operatorMetrics := operator.NewMetrics(promRegisterer)
	recorderFactory := operator.NewEventRecorderFactory(false)
	eventRecorder := recorderFactory(k8sClient, "target-allocator")

	source := fcache.NewFakeControllerSource()
	source.Add(&v1.Namespace{ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{Name: "test"}})
	source.Add(&v1.Namespace{ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
		Name: "labellednamespace",
		Labels: map[string]string{
			"label1": "label1",
		}}})

	// create the shared informer and resync every 1s
	nsMonInf := cache.NewSharedInformer(source, &v1.Namespace{}, 1*time.Second).(cache.SharedIndexInformer)

	resourceSelector, err := prometheus.NewResourceSelector(promOperatorLogger, prom, store, nsMonInf, operatorMetrics, eventRecorder)
	require.NoError(t, err)

	return &PrometheusCRWatcher{
		logger:                          slog.Default(),
		kubeMonitoringClient:            mClient,
		k8sClient:                       k8sClient,
		informers:                       informers,
		nsInformer:                      nsMonInf,
		stopChannel:                     make(chan struct{}),
		configGenerator:                 generator,
		podMonitorNamespaceSelector:     cfg.PrometheusCR.PodMonitorNamespaceSelector,
		serviceMonitorNamespaceSelector: cfg.PrometheusCR.ServiceMonitorNamespaceSelector,
		probeNamespaceSelector:          cfg.PrometheusCR.ProbeNamespaceSelector,
		scrapeConfigNamespaceSelector:   cfg.PrometheusCR.ScrapeConfigNamespaceSelector,
		resourceSelector:                resourceSelector,
		store:                           store,
		prometheusCR:                    prom,
	}, source

}

func checkCRDAvailability(ctx context.Context, client kubernetes.Interface, gvr schema.GroupVersionResource) (bool, error) {
        discoveryClient := client.Discovery()
        
        apiResourceList, err := discoveryClient.ServerResourcesForGroupVersion(gvr.GroupVersion().String())
        if err != nil {
                // If we get a NotFound error, the API group version doesn'"'"'t exist
                return false, nil
        }

        for _, resource := range apiResourceList.APIResources {
                if resource.Name == gvr.Resource {
                        return true, nil
                }
        }

        return false, nil
}

// getInformers returns a map of informers for the given resources.
// It only creates informers for CRDs that exist in the cluster.
func getInformers(ctx context.Context, logger logr.Logger, client kubernetes.Interface, factory informers.FactoriesForNamespaces) (map[string]*informers.ForResource, error) {

                return nil, err
